       3 //SYSIN    DD *                                                                 
         //******************************************************************            
         //* SYSLIN OUTPUT: THE OBJECT MODULE BEING WRITTEN TO TEMP DATA SET*            
         //*                                                                *            
         //* SYSPRINT OUTPUT: OUTPUTTING MESSAGES FROM COMPILER             *            
         //*                                                                *            
         //* SYSUT1-15 & SYSMDECK OUTPUT: DATA SETS REQUIRED BY COMPILER    *            
         //*                                                                *            
         //* SYSUDUMP OUTPUT: ENABLES STORAGE DUMPS IN CASE OF ABENDS       *            
         //******************************************************************            
       4 //SYSLIN   DD DSN=&&OBJMOD,SPACE=(CYL,(1,1)),                                   
         //            DISP=(MOD,PASS)                                                   
         //*                                                                             
       5 //SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*                                                          
         //*                                                                             
       6 //SYSUT1   DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
       7 //SYSUT2   DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
       8 //SYSUT3   DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
       9 //SYSUT4   DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))

      12 //SYSUT7   DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
      13 //SYSUT8   DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
      14 //SYSUT9   DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
      15 //SYSUT10  DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
      16 //SYSUT11  DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
      17 //SYSUT12  DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))

      19 //SYSUT14  DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
      20 //SYSUT15  DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
      21 //SYSMDECK DD SPACE=(CYL,(1,1))                                                 
         //*                                                                             
      22 //SYSUDUMP DD SYSOUT=*                                                          
         //********************************************************************          
         //* JSTEP02 WILL CREATE A LOAD MODULE, STORE IT AS A PROGRAM OBJECT  *          
         //********************************************************************          
      23 //JSTEP02  EXEC PGM=HEWL,COND=(0,LT)                                            
         //********************************************************************          
         //* SYSLIB INPUT: LOCATION OF NECESSARY IBM LIBRARIES                *          
         //*                                                                  *          
         //* SYSLIN INPUT: RECEIVING TEMP DATA SET FROM JSTEP01               *          
         //*                                                                  *          
         //* SYSLMOD OUTPUT: LOCATION OF PDSE MEMBER STORING LOAD MODULE      *          
         //*                                                                  *          
         //* SYSPRINT OUTPUT: DISPLAY RECORDS TO STANDARD OUTPUT              *          
         //*                                                                  *          
         //* SYSUDUMP OUTPUT: DUMP STORAGE IN CASE OF ABEND                   *          
         //********************************************************************          
         //*

         //*

         //*

         //*                                                                             
      27 //SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*                                                          
         //*                                                                             
      28 //SYSUDUMP DD SYSOUT=*                                                          
         //*******************************************************************           
         //* JSTEP03 FETCHES AND EXECUTES THE PROGRAM OBJECT                 *           
         //*                                                                 *           
         //* STEPLIB INPUT: LOCATION OF OUR PDSE TO STORE PROGRAM OBJECT     *           
         //*                                                                 *           
         //* COBIN INPUT: LOCATION OF FILE NEEDED FOR INPUT                  *           
         //*                                                                 *           
         //* COBOUT OUTPUT: DETERMINES WHERE OUTPUT IS SENT                  *           
         //*                                                                 *           
         //* SYSUDUMP OUTPUT: DUMPS INFO ABOUT ABENDS TO STANDARD OUTPUT     *           
         //*******************************************************************           
      29 //JSTEP03  EXEC PGM=ENDOWMT1,COND=(0,LT)

  000001               ****************************************************************                                             
  000002               * PROGRAM NAME:  ASSIGN5                                       *                                             
  000003               *                                                              *                                             
  000004               * FUNCTION:  THIS PROGRAM READS INPUT DATA RECORDS AND THEN    *                                             
  000005               *            WRITES THEM TO STANDARD OUTPUT.                   *                                             
  000006               *                                                              *                                             
  000007               * INPUT:     INFILE - THE INPUT DATA RECORDS READ IN.          *                                             
  000008               *                                                              *                                             
  000009               * OUTPUT:    OUTFILE - THE INPUT DATA RECORDS WRITTEN OUT.     *                                             
  000010               ****************************************************************                                             
  000011                                                                                                                            
  000012                IDENTIFICATION DIVISION.                                                                                    
  000013                                                                                                                            
  000014                PROGRAM-ID.    ENDOWMT1.                                                                                    
  000015                AUTHOR.        HASNAIN ATTARWALA.                                                                           
  000016                DATE-WRITTEN.  10/11/2019.                                                                                  
  000017                DATE-COMPILED. 10/20/19.                                                                                    
  000018               ****************************************************************                                             
  000019               * IT TELLS ABOUT INPUT AND OUTPUT FILES WORKIGN WITH           *                                             
  000020               * ASSIGNS INPUT/OUTPUT FILE TO IN/OUT FILES                    *                                             
  000021               ****************************************************************                                             
  000022                ENVIRONMENT DIVISION.                                                                                       
  000023               ****************************************************************                                             
  000024                INPUT-OUTPUT SECTION.                                                                                       
  000025                                                                                                                            
  000026                FILE-CONTROL.                                                                                               
  000027                                                                                                                            
  000028                    SELECT TRAN-FILE ASSIGN TO TRANFLE.                                   41                                
  000029                    SELECT LOW-ENDOWMT-FILE ASSIGN TO LEFLE.                              62                                
  000030                    SELECT REPORT-FILE ASSIGN TO RPTFLE.                                  69                                
  000031               ****************************************************************                                             
  000032                DATA DIVISION.                                                                                              
  000033               ****************************************************************                                             
  000034               * DEFINE VARIABLES NAMES FOR COBOL PROG, THEY WILL BE ASSIGNED *                                             
  000035               * TO IT WHEN FILE WILL BE READ                                 *                                             
  000036               * FD = FILE DESCRIPTOR, F = FIXED                              *                                             
  000037               * SET BUFFER OF 132 BYTES FOR WRITING A LINE                   *                                             
  000038               ****************************************************************                                             
  000039                FILE SECTION.                                                                                               
  000040                                                                                                                            
  000041                FD  TRAN-FILE                                                                                               
  000042                    RECORDING MODE IS F.                                                                                    
  000043

  000327                PROCEDURE DIVISION.                                                                                         
  000328               ****************************************************************                                             
  000329               * PARAGRAPH'S AND MATH. VERB INPUTFILE, VERB PRINT FILE        *                                             
  000330               * READ INPUT FILE CREATE LOOP, WITHIN LOOP CALL ANOTHR PARAGRAH*                                             
  000331               * DO ALL UR  MOVES, COMPUTES AND WRITE PRINT.  FINISH LOOP     *                                             
  000332               * MOVE TOTAL TO OUT TOTAL, PRINT TOTAL LINE AFTER LOOP         *                                             
  000333               * CLOSE OUTPUT FILE NOW, AND SEND FILE TO SYSOUT IN JCL BY     *                                             
  000334               * SAYING PRINT FILE                                            *                                             
  000335               * EXIT BY GO BACK, THEN EXIT EXIT FOR CONVENTION               *                                             
  000336               ****************************************************************                                             
  000337                0000-MAIN.

Context usage is indicated by the letter preceding a procedure-name reference.                                                      
These letters and their meanings are:                                                                                               
    A = ALTER (procedure-name)                                                                                                      
    D = GO TO (procedure-name) DEPENDING ON                                                                                         
    E = End of range of (PERFORM) through (procedure-name)                                                                          
    G = GO TO (procedure-name)                                                                                                      
    P = PERFORM (procedure-name)                                                                                                    
    T = (ALTER) TO PROCEED TO (procedure-name)                                                                                      
    U = USE FOR DEBUGGING (procedure-name)
